The Language of Tel'Qassir

Natively known as: Tel'qasir /tɛɭʔkjasiɹ/

Grammar

Main word order: Subject-Verb-Object-Oblique. "Mary opened the door with a key" turns into Mary opened the door with a key.
Adjective order: Adjectives are positioned after the noun.
Adposition: postpositions

Nouns

Singular Plural
Nominative No affix
ri'ei /ɹiʔɛɪ̯/ 		If ends with vowel: Suffix -na
Else: Suffix -ana

Else: Suffix -i

Else: Suffix -ini

Articles

Indefinite

The indefinite article <aen> is used only with singular, countable nouns. Otherwise, no indefinite article is applied.

Derivational morphology

Adjective → noun = If starts with vowel: Prefix ɛɪ̯n-
Else: Prefix ɛɪ̯ni-
Noun → adjective = Suffix -iɹ
Noun → verb = If starts with vowel: Prefix t-
Else: Prefix ta-
Verb → noun = Prefix ɛɪ̯-
Verb → adjective = Prefix ɭɔ-
Adjective → verb = If starts with vowel: Prefix ɸ-
Else: Prefix ɸɛɪ̯-
Adjective → adverb = Prefix da-
One who Xs (e.g. paint → painter) = Suffix -ɔɹ
Place of (e.g. wine → winery) = If starts with vowel: Prefix ɔɹs-
Else: Prefix ɔɹsa-
Diminutive = If starts with vowel: Prefix iʔ-
Else: Prefix iʔi-
Augmentative = If starts with vowel: Prefix m-
Else: Prefix ma-
